font-family:BeaufortLoL; text-transform:uppercase; font-weight:bold;"><div class="lol-navigation-item" style="padding: 4px; text-align:center; cursor:pointer"><span class="light-theme-darken" typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Taric" title="Taric"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Champion_icon.png/16px-Champion_icon.png?2d7b0" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="16" height="16" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Champion_icon.png/32px-Champion_icon.png?2d7b0 2x" data-file-width="200" data-file-height="200" /></a></span> <a href="/en-us/Taric" title="Taric">Gameplay</a></div><div class="lol-navigation-item" style="padding: 4px; <p>This page documents all known changes for <span class="inline-image label-after champion-icon" style="display:inline;white-space:pre;" data-param="" data-champion="Taric" data-skin="Original" data-game="lol"><span class="border" style="display:inline-block;position:relative;" data-width="20"><span class="mw-image-border" typeof="mw:File"><span title="An icon representing Taric"><img alt="An icon representing Taric" src="/en-us/images/thumb/Taric_OriginalSquare.png/20px-Taric_OriginalSquare.png?df987" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Taric_OriginalSquare.png/40px-Taric_OriginalSquare.png?df987 2x" data-file-width="128" data-file-height="128" /></span></span></span> <span style="white-space:normal;"><strong class="selflink">Taric</strong></span></span> in <a href="/en-us/League_of_Legends" title="League of Legends">League of Legends</a> since the champion's initial release in <a href="/en-us/V0.9.22.15" title="V0.9.22.15">V0.9.22.15</a>.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Current_version">Current version</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/en-us/Taric/Patch_history?section=1&amp;veaction=edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Current version">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/en-us/Taric/Patch_history?action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section&#039;s source code: Current version">edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<dl><dt><a href="/en-us/V14.21" title="V14.21">V14.21</a></dt></dl>
<ul><li><span class="inline-image label-after ability-icon" style="display:inline;white-space:pre;" data-param="" data-champion="Taric" data-ability="Bastion" data-game="lol"><span class="border" style="display:inline-block;position:relative;" data-width="20"><span class="mw-image-border" typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Taric#Bastion" title="An icon for Taric&#39;s ability Bastion"><img alt="An icon for Taric&#39;s ability Bastion" src="/en-us/images/thumb/Taric_Bastion.png/20px-Taric_Bastion.png?78a67" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Taric_Bastion.png/40px-Taric_Bastion.png?78a67 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></a></span></span> <span style="white-space:normal;"><a href="/en-us/Taric#Bastion" title="Taric">Bastion</a></span></span>
<ul><li>Armor ratio reduced to <span style="color:yellow; white-space:normal">6 / 7 / 8 / 9 / 10% of <b>Taric's</b> armor</span> from <span style="color:yellow; white-space:normal">9 / 10 / 11 / 12 / 13%</span>.</li></ul></li></ul>
<dl><dt><a href="/en-us/V14.20" title="V14.20">V14.20</a></dt></dl>
<ul><li><span class="inline-image label-after ability-icon" style="display:inline;white-space:pre;" data-param="" data-champion="Taric" data-ability="Bastion" data-game="lol"><span class="border" style="display:inline-block;position:relative;" data-width="20"><span class="mw-image-border" typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Taric#Bastion" title="An icon for Taric&#39;s ability Bastion"><img alt="An icon for Taric&#39;s ability Bastion" src="/en-us/images/thumb/Taric_Bastion.png/20px-Taric_Bastion.png?78a67" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Taric_Bastion.png/40px-Taric_Bastion.png?78a67 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></a></span></span> <span style="white-space:normal;"><a href="/en-us/Taric#Bastion" title="Taric">Bastion</a></span></span>
<ul><li><span class="template_sbc"><b>New Effect:</b></span> Cast now has a forgiveness radius of 175 units.</li></ul></li></ul>
<dl><dt><a href="/en-us/V14.15" title="V14.15">V14.15</a></dt></dl>
<ul><li><span class="inline-image label-after ability-icon" style="display:inline;white-space:pre;" data-param="" data-champion="Taric" data-ability="Starlight&#39;s Touch" data-game="lol"><span class="border" style="display:inline-block;position:relative;" data-width="20"><span class="mw-image-border" typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Taric#Starlight&#39;s_Touch" title="An icon for Taric&#39;s ability Starlight&#39;s Touch"><img alt="An icon for Taric&#39;s ability Starlight&#39;s Touch" src="/en-us/images/thumb/Taric_Starlight%27s_Touch.png/20px-Taric_Starlight%27s_Touch.png?8bc72" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Taric_Starlight%27s_Touch.png/40px-Taric_Starlight%27s_Touch.png?8bc72 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></a></span></span> <span style="white-space:normal;"><a href="/en-us/Taric#Starlight&#39;s_Touch" title="Taric">Starlight's Touch</a></span></span>
<ul><li><span class="template_sbc"><b>Bug Fix:</b></span> No longer fails to cast on an ally tethered by <span class="inline-image label-after ability-icon" style="display:inline;white-space:pre;" data-param="" data-champion="Taric" data-ability="Bastion" data-game="lol"><span class="border" style="display:inline-block;position:relative;" data-width="20"><span class="mw-image-border" typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Taric#Bastion" title="An icon for Taric&#39;s ability Bastion"><img alt="An icon for Taric&#39;s ability Bastion" src="/en-us/images/thumb/Taric_Bastion.png/20px-Taric_Bastion.png?78a67" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Taric_Bastion.png/40px-Taric_Bastion.png?78a67 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></a></span></span> <span style="white-space:normal;"><a href="/en-us/Taric#Bastion" title="Taric">Bastion</a></span></span> at max tether range.</li>
<li><span class="template_sbc"><b>Bug Fix:</b></span> Using <span class="inline-image item-icon label-after item-icon" style="display:inline;white-space:pre;" data-param="" data-item="Navori Flickerblade" data-game="lol"><span class="border" style="display:inline-block;position:relative;" data-width="20"><span class="mw-image-border" typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Navori_Flickerblade" title="An icon for the item Navori Flickerblade"><img alt="An icon for the item Navori Flickerblade" src="/en-us/images/thumb/Navori_Flickerblade_item.png/20px-Navori_Flickerblade_item.png?35cbf" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Navori_Flickerblade_item.png/40px-Navori_Flickerblade_item.png?35cbf 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></a></span></span> <span style="white-space:normal;"><a href="/en-us/Navori_Flickerblade" title="Navori Flickerblade">Navori Flickerblade's</a></span></span> Transcendence no longer incorrectly increases its current cooldown.</li></ul></li>
<li><span class="inline-image label-after ability-icon" style="display:inline;white-space:pre;" data-param="" data-champion="Taric" data-ability="Bastion" data-game="lol"><span class="border" style="display:inline-block;position:relative;" data-width="20"><span class="mw-image-border" typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Taric#Bastion" title="An icon for Taric&#39;s ability Bastion"><img alt="An icon for Taric&#39;s ability Bastion" src="/en-us/images/thumb/Taric_Bastion.png/20px-Taric_Bastion.png?78a67" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Taric_Bastion.png/40px-Taric_Bastion.png?78a67 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></a></span></span> <span style="white-space:normal;"><a href="/en-us/Taric#Bastion" title="Taric">Bastion</a></span></span>
<ul><li><span class="template_sbc"><b>Bug Fix:</b></span> No longer fails to cast on an ally tethered by <i>Bastion</i> at max tether range.</li>
<li><span class="template_sbc"><b>Bug Fix:</b></span> Self-casting after a previously tethered ally has died no longer seeks for ally corpse targets instead of only alive allies.</li>
<li><span class="template_sbc"><b>Bug Fix:</b></span> Tether link and unlink SFX now has a delay to prevent it from repeatedly playing when the tethered ally also repeatedly enters and exits the tether's max range.</li></ul></li></ul>
<dl><dt><a href="/en-us/V14.2" title="V14.2">V14.2</a></dt></dl>
<ul><li><span class="inline-image label-after ability-icon" style="display:inline;white-space:pre;" data-param="" data-champion="Taric" data-ability="Dazzle" data-game="lol"><span class="border" style="display:inline-block;position:relative;" data-width="20"><span class="mw-image-border" typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Taric#Dazzle" title="An icon for Taric&#39;s ability Dazzle"><img alt="An icon for Taric&#39;s ability Dazzle" src="/en-us/images/thumb/Taric_Dazzle.png/20px-Taric_Dazzle.png?4634f" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Taric_Dazzle.png/40px-Taric_Dazzle.png?4634f 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></a></span></span> <span style="white-space:normal;"><a href="/en-us/Taric#Dazzle" title="Taric">Dazzle</a></span></span>
<ul><li><span class="template_sbc"><b>New Effect:</b></span> Now grants <span class="glossary" style="white-space:pre; position:relative;" data-game="lol" data-tip="Ghosting"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Unit_collision" title="Unit collision"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Ghost.png/20px-Ghost.png?ee615" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Ghost.png/40px-Ghost.png?ee615 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></a></span> <a href="/en-us/Unit_collision" title="Unit collision">ghosting</a></span> to nearby units during the windup.</li></ul></li></ul>
<dl><dt><a href="/en-us/V14.1#January_12th_Hotfix" title="V14.1">V14.1</a> - January 12th Hotfix</dt></dl>
<ul><li>Stats
<ul><li>Armor growth reduced to 4.<small>3</small> from 4.<small>6</small>.</li></ul></li>
<li><span class="inline-image label-after ability-icon" style="display:inline;white-space:pre;" data-param="" data-champion="Taric" data-ability="Bastion" data-game="lol"><span class="border" style="display:inline-block;position:relative;" data-width="20"><span class="mw-image-border" typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Taric#Bastion" title="An icon for Taric&#39;s ability Bastion"><img alt="An icon for Taric&#39;s ability Bastion" src="/en-us/images/thumb/Taric_Bastion.png/20px-Taric_Bastion.png?78a67" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Taric_Bastion.png/40px-Taric_Bastion.png?78a67 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></a></span></span> <span style="white-space:normal;"><a href="/en-us/Taric#Bastion" title="Taric">Bastion</a></span></span>
<ul><li>Armor ratio reduced to <span style="color:yellow; white-space:normal">9 / 10 / 11 / 12 / 13% of <b>Taric's</b> armor</span> from <span style="color:yellow; white-space:normal">10 / 11 / 12 / 13 / 14%</span>.</li></ul></li></ul>
<dl><dt><a href="/en-us/V12.17" title="V12.17">V12.17</a></dt></dl>
<ul><li>Stats
<ul><li>Base magic resistance reduced to 28 from 32.</li></ul></li>
<li><span class="inline-image label-after ability-icon" style="display:inline;white-space:pre;" data-param="" data-champion="Taric" data-ability="Dazzle" data-game="lol"><span class="border" style="display:inline-block;position:relative;" data-width="20"><span class="mw-image-border" typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Taric#Dazzle" title="An icon for Taric&#39;s ability Dazzle"><img alt="An icon for Taric&#39;s ability Dazzle" src="/en-us/images/thumb/Taric_Dazzle.png/20px-Taric_Dazzle.png?4634f" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Taric_Dazzle.png/40px-Taric_Dazzle.png?4634f 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></a></span></span> <span style="white-space:normal;"><a href="/en-us/Taric#Dazzle" title="Taric">Dazzle</a></span></span>
<ul><li>Cooldown increased to 16 / 15 / 14 / 13 / 12 seconds from 15 / 14 / 13 / 12 / 11.</li></ul></li></ul>
<dl><dt><a href="/en-us/V12.11" title="V12.11">V12.11</a></dt></dl>
<ul><li><span class="inline-image label-after ability-icon" style="display:inline;white-space:pre;" data-param="" data-champion="Taric" data-ability="Starlight&#39;s Touch" data-game="lol"><span class="border" style="display:inline-block;position:relative;" data-width="20"><span class="mw-image-border" typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Taric#Starlight&#39;s_Touch" title="An icon for Taric&#39;s ability Starlight&#39;s Touch"><img alt="An icon for Taric&#39;s ability Starlight&#39;s Touch" src="/en-us/images/thumb/Taric_Starlight%27s_Touch.png/20px-Taric_Starlight%27s_Touch.png?8bc72" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Taric_Starlight%27s_Touch.png/40px-Taric_Starlight%27s_Touch.png?8bc72 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></a></span></span> <span style="white-space:normal;"><a href="/en-us/Taric#Starlight&#39;s_Touch" title="Taric">Starlight's Touch</a></span></span>
<ul><li>Heal health ratio per stack increased to <span style="color: #21B053; white-space:normal">1% of his <b>maximum</b> health</span> from <span style="color: #21B053; white-space:normal">0.<small>75</small>%</span>.</li>
<li>Mana cost reduced to 60 at all ranks from 65 / 70 / 75 / 80 / 85.</li></ul></li>

<ul><li><span class="template_sbc"><b>Bug Fix:</b></span> No longer hits everything on the map if he casts it while linked to a <span class="inline-image label-after champion-icon" style="display:inline;white-space:pre;" data-param="" data-champion="Zed" data-skin="Original" data-game="lol"><span class="border" style="display:inline-block;position:relative;" data-width="20"><span class="mw-image-border" typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Zed" title="An icon representing Zed"><img alt="An icon representing Zed" src="/en-us/images/thumb/Zed_OriginalSquare.png/20px-Zed_OriginalSquare.png?b08cd" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Zed_OriginalSquare.png/40px-Zed_OriginalSquare.png?b08cd 2x" data-file-width="128" data-file-height="128" /></a></span></span> <span style="white-space:normal;"><a href="/en-us/Zed" title="Zed">Zed</a></span></span> who's dashing to his <span class="inline-image label-after ability-icon" style="display:inline;white-space:pre;" data-param="" data-champion="Zed" data-ability="Living Shadow" data-game="lol"><span class="border" style="display:inline-block;position:relative;" data-width="20"><span class="mw-image-border" typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Zed#Living_Shadow" title="An icon for Zed&#39;s ability Living Shadow"><img alt="An icon for Zed&#39;s ability Living Shadow" src="/en-us/images/thumb/Zed_Living_Shadow.png/20px-Zed_Living_Shadow.png?20068" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Zed_Living_Shadow.png/40px-Zed_Living_Shadow.png?20068 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></a></span></span> <span style="white-space:normal;"><a href="/en-us/Zed#Living_Shadow" title="Zed">Living Shadow</a></span></span>.</li></ul></li></ul>

<ul><li><span class="template_sbc"><b>Bug Fix:</b></span> Fixed a bug where it was granting more armor than intended.</li></ul></li>
<li><span class="inline-image label-after ability-icon" style="display:inline;white-space:pre;" data-param="" data-champion="Taric" data-ability="Dazzle" data-game="lol"><span class="border" style="display:inline-block;position:relative;" data-width="20"><span class="mw-image-border" typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Taric#Dazzle" title="An icon for Taric&#39;s ability Dazzle"><img alt="An icon for Taric&#39;s ability Dazzle" src="/en-us/images/thumb/Taric_Dazzle.png/20px-Taric_Dazzle.png?4634f" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Taric_Dazzle.png/40px-Taric_Dazzle.png?4634f 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></a></span></span> <span style="white-space:normal;"><a href="/en-us/Taric#Dazzle" title="Taric">Dazzle</a></span></span>
<ul><li>Base damage reduced to 90 / 130 / 170 / 210 / 250 from 105 / 150 / 195 / 240 / 285.</li>
<li>Bonus armor ratio increased to <span style="color:yellow; white-space:normal">50% <b>bonus</b> armor</span> from <span style="color:yellow; white-space:normal">30%</span>.</li></ul></li>

<dl><dt><a href="/en-us/V7.14" title="V7.14">V7.14</a></dt></dl>
<ul><li>Stats
<ul><li>Base mana regeneration increased to 8.<small>5</small> from 5.</li>
<li>Mana regeneration growth reduced to 0.<small>8</small> from 1.</li></ul></li>
<li><span class="inline-image label-after ability-icon" style="display:inline;white-space:pre;" data-param="" data-champion="Taric" data-ability="Starlight&#39;s Touch" data-game="lol"><span class="border" style="display:inline-block;position:relative;" data-width="20"><span class="mw-image-border" typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Taric#Starlight&#39;s_Touch" title="An icon for Taric&#39;s ability Starlight&#39;s Touch"><img alt="An icon for Taric&#39;s ability Starlight&#39;s Touch" src="/en-us/images/thumb/Taric_Starlight%27s_Touch.png/20px-Taric_Starlight%27s_Touch.png?8bc72" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Taric_Starlight%27s_Touch.png/40px-Taric_Starlight%27s_Touch.png?8bc72 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></a></span></span> <span style="white-space:normal;"><a href="/en-us/Taric#Starlight&#39;s_Touch" title="Taric">Starlight's Touch</a></span></span>
<ul><li>Base heal per charge changed to 30 at all ranks from 20 / 30 / 40 / 50 / 60.</li>
<li>Health ratio per charge changed to <span style="color: #21B053; white-space:normal">1% <b>maximum</b> health</span> from <span style="color: #21B053; white-space:normal">1.<small>5</small>% <b>bonus</b> health</span>.</li>
<li>Maximum charges changed to 1 / 2 / 3 / 4 / 5 from 3 at all ranks.</li>
<li>Mana cost changed to 70 / 80 / 90 / 100 / 110 from 60 / 80 / 100 / 120 / 140.</li>
<li><span class="template_sbc"><b>New Effect:</b></span> Now has a 3 second cooldown. <i>Recharge time unchanged.</i></li>
<li><span class="template_sbc"><b>Removed:</b></span> <span class="inline-image label-after ability-icon" style="display:inline;white-space:pre;" data-param="" data-champion="Taric" data-ability="Bravado" data-game="lol"><span class="border" style="display:inline-block;position:relative;" data-width="20"><span class="mw-image-border" typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Taric#Bravado" title="An icon for Taric&#39;s ability Bravado"><img alt="An icon for Taric&#39;s ability Bravado" src="/en-us/images/thumb/Taric_Bravado.png/20px-Taric_Bravado.png?732b9" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Taric_Bravado.png/40px-Taric_Bravado.png?732b9 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></a></span></span> <span style="white-space:normal;"><a href="/en-us/Taric#Bravado" title="Taric">Bravado</a></span></span> empowered attacks reduces <i>Starlight's Touch's</i> recharge timer.</li>
<li><span class="template_sbc"><b>New Effect:</b></span> <span class="inline-image label-after ability-icon" style="display:inline;white-space:pre;" data-param="" data-champion="Taric" data-ability="Bravado" data-game="lol"><span class="border" style="display:inline-block;position:relative;" data-width="20"><span class="mw-image-border" typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Taric#Bravado" title="An icon for Taric&#39;s ability Bravado"><img alt="An icon for Taric&#39;s ability Bravado" src="/en-us/images/thumb/Taric_Bravado.png/20px-Taric_Bravado.png?732b9" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Taric_Bravado.png/40px-Taric_Bravado.png?732b9 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></a></span></span> <span style="white-space:normal;"><a href="/en-us/Taric#Bravado" title="Taric">Bravado</a></span></span> empowered attacks now grant 1 charge of <i>Starlight's Touch</i> and reduce <i>Starlight's Touch's</i> cooldown by 1 second.</li></ul></li>

<li>Cooldown changed to 17 / 16 / 15 / 14 / 13 seconds from 15 at all ranks.</li>
<li>Stun duration changed to 1.<small>25</small> seconds at all ranks from 1 / 1.<small>125</small> / 1.<small>25</small> / 1.<small>375</small> / 1.<small>5</small>.</li></ul></li></ul>

<li>Base mana regeneration reduced to 5 from 8.<small>5</small>.</li>
<li>Base armor reduced to 25 from 25.<small>876</small>.</li>
<li>Base attack damage reduced to 55 from 57.<small>88</small>.</li>
<li>Mana growth increased to 75 from 56.</li>
<li>Mana regeneration growth increased to 1 from 0.<small>8</small>.</li>
<li>Armor growth reduced to 3.<small>4</small> from 3.<small>7</small>.</li></ul></li>

white-space:normal">(+ 60% AP)</span> <span style="color: #21B053; white-space:normal">(+ 4.<small>5</small>% <b>bonus</b> health)</span>. <span class="inline-image label-after ability-icon" style="display:inline;white-space:pre;" data-param="" data-champion="Taric" data-ability="Bravado" data-game="lol"><span class="border" style="display:inline-block;position:relative;" data-width="20"><span class="mw-image-border" typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Taric#Bravado" title="An icon for Taric&#39;s ability Bravado"><img alt="An icon for Taric&#39;s ability Bravado" src="/en-us/images/thumb/Taric_Bravado.png/20px-Taric_Bravado.png?732b9" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Taric_Bravado.png/40px-Taric_Bravado.png?732b9 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></a></span></span> <span style="white-space:normal;"><a href="/en-us/Taric#Bravado" title="Taric">Bravado's</a></span></span> on-hit cooldown reduction is increased to <span class="pp-tooltip" style="position:relative; After that time, the beams erupt dealing 60 / 105 / 150 / 195 / 240 <span style="color: #7A6DFF; white-space:normal">(+ 50% AP)</span> <span style="color:yellow; white-space:normal">(+ 30% <b>bonus</b> armor)</span> magic damage to enemies hit and stunning them for 1 / 1.<small>125</small> / 1.<small>25</small> / 1.<small>375</small> / 1.<small>5</small> seconds.</li>

<li>Enemy armor reduction reduced to 5 / 10 / 15 / 20 / 25 from 10 / 15 / 20 / 25 / 30.</li>
<li>Enemy armor reduction armor ratio reduced to <span style="color:yellow; white-space:normal">5% armor</span> from <span style="color:yellow; white-space:normal">10% armor</span></li></ul></li>

<ul><li><span class="inline-image label-after ability-icon" style="display:inline;white-space:pre;" data-param="" data-champion="Taric" data-ability="Imbue" data-game="lol"><span class="border" style="display:inline-block;position:relative;" data-width="20"><span class="mw-image-border" typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Taric#Imbue" title="An icon for Taric&#39;s ability Imbue"><img alt="An icon for Taric&#39;s ability Imbue" src="/en-us/images/thumb/Taric_Imbue.png/20px-Taric_Imbue.png?372c4" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Taric_Imbue.png/40px-Taric_Imbue.png?372c4 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></a></span></span> <span style="white-space:normal;"><a href="/en-us/Taric#Imbue" title="Taric">Imbue</a></span></span>
<ul><li>Base heal reduced to 70 / 120 / 170 / 220 / 270 from 90 / 135 / 180 / 225 / 270.</li></ul></li>
<li><span class="inline-image label-after ability-icon" style="display:inline;white-space:pre;" data-param="" data-champion="Taric" data-ability="Radiance" data-game="lol"><span class="border" style="display:inline-block;position:relative;" data-width="20"><span class="mw-image-border" typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Taric#Radiance" title="An icon for Taric&#39;s ability Radiance"><img alt="An icon for Taric&#39;s ability Radiance" src="/en-us/images/thumb/Taric_Radiance.png/20px-Taric_Radiance.png?34582" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Taric_Radiance.png/40px-Taric_Radiance.png?34582 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></a></span></span> <span style="white-space:normal;"><a href="/en-us/Taric#Radiance" title="Taric">Radiance</a></span></span>
<ul><li>Cooldown increased to 20 seconds from 15.</li></ul></li></ul>
<dl><dt><a href="/en-us/V0.9.22.16" title="V0.9.22.16">V0.9.22.16</a></dt></dl>
<ul><li><span class="inline-image label-after ability-icon" style="display:inline;white-space:pre;" data-param="" data-champion="Taric" data-ability="Imbue" data-game="lol"><span class="border" style="display:inline-block;position:relative;" data-width="20"><span class="mw-image-border" typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Taric#Imbue" title="An icon for Taric&#39;s ability Imbue"><img alt="An icon for Taric&#39;s ability Imbue" src="/en-us/images/thumb/Taric_Imbue.png/20px-Taric_Imbue.png?372c4" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Taric_Imbue.png/40px-Taric_Imbue.png?372c4 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></a></span></span> <span style="white-space:normal;"><a href="/en-us/Taric#Imbue" title="Taric">Imbue</a></span></span>
<ul><li>Base heal increased to 90 / 135 / 180 / 225 / 270 from 90 / 130 / 170 / 210 / 240.</li>
<li>Bonus self heal increased to 40% from 25%.</li>
<li>On-hit cooldown reduction reduced to 2 seconds from 2 / 2.<small>25</small> / 2.<small>5</small> / 2.<small>75</small> / 3.</li>
<li>Cooldown reduced to 20 / 19 / 18 / 17 / 16 seconds from 20 at all ranks.</li></ul></li>
<li><span class="inline-image label-after ability-icon" style="display:inline;white-space:pre;" data-param="" data-champion="Taric" data-ability="Shatter" data-game="lol"><span class="border" style="display:inline-block;position:relative;" data-width="20"><span class="mw-image-border" typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Taric#Shatter" title="An icon for Taric&#39;s ability Shatter"><img alt="An icon for Taric&#39;s ability Shatter" src="/en-us/images/thumb/Taric_Shatter.png/20px-Taric_Shatter.png?39d58" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Taric_Shatter.png/40px-Taric_Shatter.png?39d58 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></a></span></span> <span style="white-space:normal;"><a href="/en-us/Taric#Shatter" title="Taric">Shatter</a></span></span>
<ul><li><span class="template_sbc"><b>New Effect:</b></span> Always gives <b>Taric</b> <span style="color:yellow; white-space:normal">10 / 15 / 20 / 25 / 30 <b>bonus</b> armor</span> regardless of cooldown.</li>
<li><span class="template_sbc"><b>New Effect:</b></span> While off cooldown <b>Taric</b> emits an aura giving him and his allies <span style="color:yellow; white-space:normal">10 / 15 / 20 / 25 / 30 <b>bonus</b> armor</span>.</li>
<li><span class="template_sbc"><b>New Effect:</b></span> Enemy targets have their <span style="color:yellow; white-space:normal">armor reduced by 10 / 15 / 20 / 25 / 30</span>.</li></ul></li>
<li><span class="inline-image label-after ability-icon" style="display:inline;white-space:pre;" data-param="" data-champion="Taric" data-ability="Dazzle" data-game="lol"><span class="border" style="display:inline-block;position:relative;" data-width="20"><span class="mw-image-border" typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Taric#Dazzle" title="An icon for Taric&#39;s ability Dazzle"><img alt="An icon for Taric&#39;s ability Dazzle" src="/en-us/images/thumb/Taric_Dazzle.png/20px-Taric_Dazzle.png?4634f" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Taric_Dazzle.png/40px-Taric_Dazzle.png?4634f 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></a></span></span> <span style="white-space:normal;"><a href="/en-us/Taric#Dazzle" title="Taric">Dazzle</a></span></span>
<ul><li>Cooldown increased to 14 / 13 / 12 / 11 / 10 seconds from 13 / 12 / 11 / 10 / 9.</li>
<li><span class="template_sbc"><b>New Effect:</b></span> Does more damage the closer <b>Taric</b> is to his target.</li>
<li>Base damage increased to 80 / 160 / 240 / 320 / 400 from 80 / 130 / 180 / 230 / 280.</li>
<li>Maximum stun duration reduced to 2 seconds from 2.<small>5</small>.</li>
<li>Tooltip updated.</li></ul></li>
<li><span class="inline-image label-after ability-icon" style="display:inline;white-space:pre;" data-param="" data-champion="Taric" data-ability="Radiance" data-game="lol"><span class="border" style="display:inline-block;position:relative;" data-width="20"><span class="mw-image-border" typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Taric#Radiance" title="An icon for Taric&#39;s ability Radiance"><img alt="An icon for Taric&#39;s ability Radiance" src="/en-us/images/thumb/Taric_Radiance.png/20px-Taric_Radiance.png?34582" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Taric_Radiance.png/40px-Taric_Radiance.png?34582 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></a></span></span> <span style="white-space:normal;"><a href="/en-us/Taric#Radiance" title="Taric">Radiance</a></span></span>
<ul><li>Mana cost changed to 10 + 10 / 15 / 20 per second active.</li>
<li>Cast time changed to instant.</li>
<li>Tooltip updated.</li></ul></li></ul>
<dl><dt><a href="/en-us/V0.9.22.15" title="V0.9.22.15">V0.9.22.15</a></dt></dl>
<ul><li>Added</li></ul>

</td></tr></tbody></table><table style="width:100%;"><tbody><tr><td style="vertical-align:top; padding: 0.5em; text-align: left;"><span class="template_sbc"><b>Active:</b></span> <span class="inline-image label-after champion-icon" style="display:inline;white-space:pre;" data-param="" data-champion="Taric" data-skin="Original" data-game="lol"><span class="border" style="display:inline-block;position:relative;" data-width="20"><span class="mw-image-border" typeof="mw:File"><span title="An icon representing Taric"><img alt="An icon representing Taric" src="/en-us/images/thumb/Taric_OriginalSquare.png/20px-Taric_OriginalSquare.png?df987" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Taric_OriginalSquare.png/40px-Taric_OriginalSquare.png?df987 2x" data-file-width="128" data-file-height="128" /></span></span></span> <span style="white-space:normal;"><strong class="selflink">Taric</strong></span></span> calls down a star that descends to him over a short time. In addition to granting <span class="glossary" style="white-space:pre; position:relative;" data-game="lol" data-tip="Untargetability"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Untargetable" title="Untargetable"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Untargetable_icon.png/20px-Untargetable_icon.png?c022c" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Untargetable_icon.png/40px-Untargetable_icon.png?c022c 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></a></span> <a href="/en-us/Untargetable" class="mw-redirect" title="Untargetable">untargetability</a></span>, <b>vanish</b> briefly hides a unit from the game's renderer, which causes it to become completely undetectable and invisible even to effects such as <span class="inline-image item-icon label-after item-icon" style="display:inline;white-space:pre;" data-param="" data-item="Oracle Lens" data-game="lol"><span class="border" style="display:inline-block;position:relative;" data-width="20"><span class="mw-image-border" typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Oracle_Lens" title="An icon for the item Oracle Lens"><img alt="An icon for the item Oracle Lens" src="/en-us/images/thumb/Oracle_Lens_item.png/20px-Oracle_Lens_item.png?526ae" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Oracle_Lens_item.png/40px-Oracle_Lens_item.png?526ae 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></a></span></span> <span style="white-space:normal;"><a href="/en-us/Oracle_Lens" title="Oracle Lens">Oracle Lens</a></span></span>. <b>Vanished</b> units are <span class="glossary" style="white-space:pre; position:relative;" data-game="lol" data-tip="Lockout"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Terminology#Lockout" title="Terminology"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Lockout_icon_2.png/20px-Lockout_icon_2.png?5e81e" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Lockout_icon_2.png/40px-Lockout_icon_2.png?5e81e 2x" data-file-width="44" data-file-height="44" /></a></span> <a href="/en-us/Terminology#Lockout" title="Terminology">unable to act</a></span>. As with all untargetability, <span class="glossary" style="white-space:pre; position:relative;" data-game="lol" data-tip="Tether"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Tether" title="Tether"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Karma_Focused_Resolve.png/20px-Karma_Focused_Resolve.png?3ca72" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Karma_Focused_Resolve.png/40px-Karma_Focused_Resolve.png?3ca72 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></a></span> <a href="/en-us/Tether" title="Tether">tethers</a></span> will still persist on a target that <i>vanishes</i>.<hr style="width:90%; border:solid rgba(255,255,255,0.25); border-width:0px 0px 1px 0px;" />
<p>
<b>Vanish</b> is not considered <span class="glossary" style="white-space:pre; position:relative;" data-game="lol" data-tip="Stealth"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Stealth" title="Stealth"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Teemo_Guerrilla_Warfare.png/20px-Teemo_Guerrilla_Warfare.png?116ff" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Teemo_Guerrilla_Warfare.png/40px-Teemo_Guerrilla_Warfare.png?116ff 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></a></span> <a href="/en-us/Stealth" title="Stealth">stealth</a></span> and does not interact with <span class="glossary" style="white-space:pre; position:relative;" data-game="lol" data-tip="Sight"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Sight" title="Sight"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Sight_icon.png/20px-Sight_icon.png?0aaf0" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/Sight_icon.png?0aaf0 2x" data-file-width="26" data-file-height="26" /></a></span> <a href="/en-us/Sight" title="Sight">sight</a></span> effects.</p>

<div style="text-align:center; font-size:0.9em; font-weight:bold; margin-top:4px; margin-bottom:4px;"><div style="background:#163474; color:#CCC;line-height:15px; padding:5px 0 5px 0; border-radius:2px;"><div style="display:inline; vertical-align:middle;"><span typeof="mw:File"><span><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png/20px-League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png?c4f67" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="21" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png/40px-League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png?c4f67 2x" data-file-width="49" data-file-height="52" /></span></span></div> League of Legends content</div></div><a href="/en-us/Template:Data_Taric/Gemcraft?action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Template:Data Taric/Gemcraft (page does not exist)">Template:Data Taric/Gemcraft</a></div><div class="blue-tooltip" style="width:500px;box-sizing:content-box;">
<div style="text-align:center; font-size:0.9em; font-weight:bold; margin-top:4px; margin-bottom:4px;"><div style="background:#163474; color:#CCC;line-height:15px; padding:5px 0 5px 0; border-radius:2px;"><div style="display:inline; vertical-align:middle;"><span typeof="mw:File"><span><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png/20px-League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png?c4f67" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="21" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png/40px-League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png?c4f67 2x" data-file-width="49" data-file-height="52" /></span></span></div> League of Legends content</div></div><div class="abilitytooltip blurb skill skill_w" style="overflow:hidden; position:relative; line-height: 20px;">
<table width="100%" style="border-bottom: 1px solid rgba(255,255,255,0.25);">
<tbody><tr>
<td style="font-size:140%; color: #9797fc; font-weight:bold; text-shadow: 0 2px black; padding-right:14px;"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Template:Data_Taric/Bastion" title="Template:Data Taric/Bastion"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Taric_Bastion.png/48px-Taric_Bastion.png?78a67" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="48" height="48" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/Taric_Bastion.png?78a67 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></a></span>&#8194;Bastion
</td>
<td style="text-align:right;"><span style="color: #9797fc; font-weight:bold;">COOLDOWN:</span> 15
</td></tr></tbody></table><table style="width:100%;"><tbody><tr><td style="vertical-align:top; padding: 0.5em; text-align: left;"><span class="template_sbc"><b>Passive:</b></span> <span class="inline-image label-after champion-icon" style="display:inline;white-space:pre;" data-param="" data-champion="Taric" data-skin="Original" data-game="lol"><span class="border" style="display:inline-block;position:relative;" data-width="20"><span class="mw-image-border" typeof="mw:File"><span title="An icon representing Taric"><img alt="An icon representing Taric" src="/en-us/images/thumb/Taric_OriginalSquare.png/20px-Taric_OriginalSquare.png?df987" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Taric_OriginalSquare.png/40px-Taric_OriginalSquare.png?df987 2x" data-file-width="128" data-file-height="128" /></span></span></span> <span style="white-space:normal;"><strong class="selflink">Taric</strong></span></span> gains <span style="white-space:nowrap"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Armor" title="Armor"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Armor_icon.png/15px-Armor_icon.png?393ad" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="15" height="15" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Armor_icon.png/30px-Armor_icon.png?393ad 2x" data-file-width="72" data-file-height="72" /></a></span>&#160;<span style="color:yellow; white-space:normal"><b>bonus</b> armor</span></span> and forms a <span class="glossary" style="white-space:pre; position:relative;" data-game="lol" data-tip="Tether"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Tether" title="Tether"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Karma_Focused_Resolve.png/20px-Karma_Focused_Resolve.png?3ca72" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Karma_Focused_Resolve.png/40px-Karma_Focused_Resolve.png?3ca72 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></a></span> <a href="/en-us/Tether" title="Tether">tether</a></span> to the ally bound by <i>Bastion</i>. While the tether persists, the ally gains the <span style="color:yellow; white-space:normal"><b>bonus</b> armor</span> and <b>Taric's</b> abilities are mimicked to them.</td></tr><tr><td style="vertical-align:top; padding: 0.5em; text-align: left;"><span class="template_sbc"><b>Active:</b></span> <b>Taric</b> <span class="glossary" style="white-space:pre; position:relative;" data-game="lol" data-tip="Shields"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Shield" title="Shield"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Hybrid_resistances_icon.png/20px-Hybrid_resistances_icon.png?18138" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Hybrid_resistances_icon.png/40px-Hybrid_resistances_icon.png?18138 2x" data-file-width="121" data-file-height="121" /></a></span> <a href="/en-us/Shield" title="Shield">shields</a></span> himself and the target allied champion for a short time, with the amount based on each <span style="color: #21B053; white-space:normal">target's <b>maximum</b> health</span>. He also binds them with <i>Bastion</i>.</td></tr><tr><td style="vertical-align:top; padding: 0.5em; text-align: left;"><b>Taric</b> can also <a href="/en-us/Self-targeted" title="Self-targeted">self-cast</a> to shield himself.</td></tr><tr><td style="vertical-align:top; padding: 0.5em; text-align: left;"><hr style="border:solid rgba(255,255,255,0.25); border-width:0px 0px 1px 0px;" />Only one ally can be bound at a time, and selecting a new ally overrides the previous bind.</td></tr></tbody></table></div></div><div class="blue-tooltip" style="width:500px;box-sizing:content-box;"><div style="line-height:14px; padding:5px 0 5px 0; text-align:center; color:#CCC; background:#A00; border-radius:2px; font-size:12px; font-weight:bold; margin-top:4px; margin-bottom:4px;">Removed content</div>
<div style="text-align:center; font-size:0.9em; font-weight:bold; margin-top:4px; margin-bottom:4px;"><div style="background:#163474; color:#CCC;line-height:15px; padding:5px 0 5px 0; border-radius:2px;"><div style="display:inline; vertical-align:middle;"><span typeof="mw:File"><span><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png/20px-League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png?c4f67" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="21" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png/40px-League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png?c4f67 2x" data-file-width="49" data-file-height="52" /></span></span></div> League of Legends content</div></div><a href="/en-us/Template:Data_Taric/Imbue?action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Template:Data Taric/Imbue (page does not exist)">Template:Data Taric/Imbue</a></div><div class="blue-tooltip" style="width:500px;box-sizing:content-box;"><div style="line-height:14px; padding:5px 0 5px 0; text-align:center; color:#CCC; background:#A00; border-radius:2px; font-size:12px; font-weight:bold; margin-top:4px; margin-bottom:4px;">Removed content</div>
<div style="text-align:center; font-size:0.9em; font-weight:bold; margin-top:4px; margin-bottom:4px;"><div style="background:#163474; color:#CCC;line-height:15px; padding:5px 0 5px 0; border-radius:2px;"><div style="display:inline; vertical-align:middle;"><span typeof="mw:File"><span><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png/20px-League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png?c4f67" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="21" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png/40px-League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png?c4f67 2x" data-file-width="49" data-file-height="52" /></span></span></div> League of Legends content</div></div><a href="/en-us/Template:Data_Taric/Shatter?action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Template:Data Taric/Shatter (page does not exist)">Template:Data Taric/Shatter</a></div><div class="blue-tooltip" style="width:500px;box-sizing:content-box;"><div style="line-height:14px; padding:5px 0 5px 0; text-align:center; color:#CCC; background:#A00; border-radius:2px; font-size:12px; font-weight:bold; margin-top:4px; margin-bottom:4px;">Removed content</div>
<div style="text-align:center; font-size:0.9em; font-weight:bold; margin-top:4px; margin-bottom:4px;"><div style="background:#163474; color:#CCC;line-height:15px; padding:5px 0 5px 0; border-radius:2px;"><div style="display:inline; vertical-align:middle;"><span typeof="mw:File"><span><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png/20px-League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png?c4f67" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="21" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png/40px-League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png?c4f67 2x" data-file-width="49" data-file-height="52" /></span></span></div> League of Legends content</div></div><a href="/en-us/Template:Data_Taric/Radiance?action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Template:Data Taric/Radiance (page does not exist)">Template:Data Taric/Radiance</a></div><div class="blue-tooltip" style=""><div style="text-align:center; font-size:0.9em; font-weight:bold; margin-top:4px; margin-bottom:4px;"><div style="background:#163474; color:#CCC;line-height:15px; padding:5px 0 5px 0; border-radius:2px;"><div style="display:inline; vertical-align:middle;"><span typeof="mw:File"><span><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png/20px-League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png?c4f67" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="21" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png/40px-League_of_Legends_icon_nav.png?c4f67 2x" data-file-width="49" data-file-height="52" /></span></span></div> League of Legends content</div></div><div style="width: 550px; margin:5px;"><div style="margin-bottom:5px; border-bottom: 1px solid rgba(255,255,255,0.25);"><span typeof="mw:File"><span><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Grievous_Wounds_icon.png/44px-Grievous_Wounds_icon.png?053fa" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="44" height="44" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/Grievous_Wounds_icon.png?053fa 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></span></span> <span class="tooltip-header" style="font-size: 140%; font-weight: bold;">Grievous Wounds</span></div>
<b>Grievous Wounds</b> is a debuff that reduces self-healing, incoming healing, and health regeneration by 40%.<hr style="width:90%; border:solid rgba(255,255,255,0.25); border-width:0px 0px 1px 0px;" />
<p>
<b>Grievous Wounds</b> does not <a href="/en-us/Stack" title="Stack">stack</a>, the duration of the <i>debuff</i> will overlap on separate effects and refresh on the same effect.</p>
</div></div></div>
